; flashes a graphics

8EAE   29 01                AND #$01

;
;   calculate HGR line address A (bits abcdefgh => address  010fghcd eabab000 )
8EDA   48         L8EDA     PHA
8EDB   29 C0                AND #$C0    ; keep bits 6 & 7 only
8EDD   85 5E                STA $5E
8EDF   4A                   LSR A
8EE0   4A                   LSR A
8EE1   05 5E                ORA $5E     ; duplicate them in bits 4 & 5
8EE3   85 5E                STA $5E
8EE5   68                   PLA
8EE6   85 5F                STA $5F     ; duplicate bits 0-7 in 8-15
8EE8   0A                   ASL A       ; get rid of bits 6 & 7
8EE9   0A                   ASL A
8EEA   0A                   ASL A       ; shift bit 5 into MSB
8EEB   26 5F                ROL $5F
8EED   0A                   ASL A       ; and bit 4 too
8EEE   26 5F                ROL $5F
8EF0   0A                   ASL A       ; bit 3 becomes bit 7
8EF1   66 5E                ROR $5E
8EF3   A5 5F                LDA $5F
8EF5   29 1F                AND #$1F
8EF7   09 40                ORA #$40
8EF9   85 5F                STA $5F
8EFB   60                   RTS

A4EA   F0 E8                BEQ LA4D4                    => increment depth if N & 7 = 0,
A4EC   A9 04                LDA #$04                     => decrement depth if N & 7 # 0 (and skip 4 bytes)
A4EE   20 FD A4             JSR LA4FD       ; skip 4 bytes

A4F2   D0 E1                BNE LA4D5       ; still in the same branch, continue

; GCR 6-and-2 encoding :
; - take the two least-significant bits of all the 256 bytes of buffer pointed by ($3E) and group them by 6 at BC00-BC55
; - put  the six  most-significant bits of all the 256 bytes of buffer pointed by ($3E) at BB00-BBFF
